## âœï¸ SECTION 5: AD COPY EXAMPLES

### 5.1 Thai Ad Copy

#### Copy 1: Investment Hook (à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸šà¸™à¸±à¸à¸¥à¸‡à¸—à¸¸à¸™)

Q: Can foreigners buy this property?
A: Yes! Foreigners can own condominiums in Thailand with 100% freehold
   ownership in their own name. No company structure required.
   Foreign quota limit: 49% of total units (we have quota available).

Q: What documents do I need?
A: Required documents for foreign buyers:
   â€¢ Valid passport
   â€¢ Proof of funds transfer from overseas (FET form)
   â€¢ Proof of address (in some cases)
   Our team will guide you through the entire process.

Q: When will it be completed?
A: Currently 35% complete. Expected completion and transfer: Q2/2029
   (approximately 3 years from now)

Q: What's included in "fully fitted"?
A: Your unit comes with:
   â€¢ Built-in kitchen with countertop and sink
   â€¢ Built-in wardrobes
   â€¢ Bathroom fixtures complete
   â€¢ Basic appliances (air conditioning, water heater)
   â€¢ Ready to move in â€” just bring your personal items!

Q: What are the monthly fees?
A: â€¢ Common area fee: à¸¿50/sqm/month (~$1.40/sqm)
   â€¢ Sinking fund: à¸¿500/sqm (one-time payment at transfer)
   
   Example for 30sqm studio:
   â€¢ Monthly: ~à¸¿1,500 ($42)
   â€¢ Sinking fund: à¸¿15,000 ($420 one-time)

Q: Why is this location good for rental?
A: This is one of Pattaya's best rental locations because:
   â€¢ The Avenue = Major tourist & expat destination
   â€¢ Soi Buakhao = High concentration of long-term expats
   â€¢ Walking distance to everything = Very attractive to renters
   â€¢ Year-round demand from international tenants
   â€¢ Proven rental track record in this area

Q: Is there property management?
A: [Answer based on actual project info â€” if yes, describe services;
    if no, can recommend third-party management companies]

Q: Can I get a mortgage?
A: Financing options:
   â€¢ Thai banks: Available for foreigners (typically 50-70% LTV)
   â€¢ Requirements: Work permit or long-term visa
   â€¢ Our team can introduce you to bank partners
   â€¢ Developer payment plan: 30-month installments during construction

Q: What if I want to sell before completion?
A: You can transfer your contract to another buyer (assignment).
   â€¢ Requires developer approval
   â€¢ You may profit if property value increases
   â€¢ Common practice in pre-construction properties
